<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срабатывать.html>сраба́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">srabátyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сработать.html>срабо́тать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to work, to function <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a machine</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to succeed, to work (of an attempt)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make, to produce</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сражение.html>сраже́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sražénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сражение.html>сраже́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сражение.html>сраже́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сражение.html>сраже́ний</a></b>)

***сразить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сразить.html>срази́ть</a> (11859)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разить.html>рази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сразить.html>срази́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">srazítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сража́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to strike, to hit, to smite</li>
<li>to strike down, to defeat, to crush</li></ol>

***сразу.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сразу.html>сра́зу</a> (172)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>ра́зу</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rázu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, unexpectedly in the dative case (possibly an archaism).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сразу.html>сра́зу</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">srázu</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>at once, simultaneously</li>
<li>at one stroke</li>
<li>at once, right away, straight away
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1886</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Chekhov</a>,  “хори́стка  | The Chorus Girl | ”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span> |  republished in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>Русский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></cite>, 2002:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:барыня.html>ба́рыня</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сразу.html>сра́зу</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответить.html>отве́тила</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Bárynja ne <b>srázu</b> otvétila.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The lady did not answer <b>right away</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>straight off, out of hand</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***срам.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>срам</a> (14623)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">срамъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sramŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sormъ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сор.html>соро́м</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soróm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>срам</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sram</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срам.html>сра́ма</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>shame, disgrace</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:срастаться.html>сраста́ться</a> (26736)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срастись.html>срасти́сь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">srastísʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срастаться.html>сраста́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">srastátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срастись.html>срасти́сь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to accrete, to grow together, to knit <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of bones</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to inosculate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of fibers, blood vessels</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сломанный.html>сло́манная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кость.html>кость</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:срастаться.html>сраста́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">slómannaja kostʹ xorošó <b>srastájetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the broken bone is knitting well</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to merge, to fuse, to coalesce, to interpenetrate</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расти.html>расти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срастись.html>срасти́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">srastísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срастаться.html>сраста́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to accrete, to grow together, to knit <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of bones</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to inosculate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of fibers, blood vessels</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сломанный.html>сло́манная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кость.html>кость</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:срастись.html>сросла́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">slómannaja kostʹ xorošó <b>sroslásʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the broken bone (has) knitted well</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to merge, to fuse, to coalesce, to interpenetrate</li></ol>

***среда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:среда.html>среда́</a> (1685)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">срѣда</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">srěda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*serda</i>. Displaced native <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:середа.html>середа́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sereda</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">middle; Wednesday</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (cf. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:середа.html>середа́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">seredá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">третииникъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tretiinikŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Wednesday</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">third (day)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:среда.html>среда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sredá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:среда.html>среды́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:среда.html>сре́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:среда.html>сре́д</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Wednesday
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:среда.html>сре́ду</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>srédu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on Wednesday</span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:среда.html>среды́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">so <b>sredý</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from Wednesday</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:среда.html>среды́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тницы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">so <b>sredý</b> do pjátnicy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">from Wednesday to Friday</span></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:срединный.html>среди́нный</a> (24792)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">среди́на</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sredína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срединный.html>среди́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sredínnyj</span>) (<i>rare comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)среди́ннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)среди́нней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> middle, located in the middle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> average, ordinary, commonplace</li></ol>
